## @Entropy-pp

题目是：Transparent SNARKs over Galois Rings

## Copilot

感谢你提供论文标题！**"Transparent SNARKs over Galois Rings"**（ePrint 2025/263）是一篇关于密码学中 SNARK（简洁非交互式知识论证）构造的论文，将 SNARK 技术扩展到 **Galois 环**（而非传统的有限域）上。

虽然我无法直接阅读该 PDF，但我可以根据标题和主题为你提供一些背景信息：

---

### 📖 主题概述

- **SNARKs (Succinct Non-interactive Arguments of Knowledge)**：一种密码学证明系统，允许证明者向验证者简洁地证明某个计算的正确性，而无需透露底层数据。
- **Transparent**：指不需要可信设置（trusted setup），所有参数都是公开可验证的（例如基于哈希函数或随机预言机）。
- **Galois Rings**：是有限域（Galois Fields）的推广，形如 $\mathbb{Z}_{p^k}[x]/(f(x))$，在编码理论和多方计算（MPC）中有重要应用。传统 SNARK 通常构建在有限域上，将其推广到 Galois 环上可能带来效率优势或新的应用场景。

### 🔑 可能的研究贡献

- 在 Galois 环上构造透明 SNARK 协议
- 处理环上零因子（zero divisors）等带来的技术挑战
- 可能利用环结构获得更好的效率（例如利用 $\mathbb{Z}_{2^k}$ 与机器字长的天然对齐）
- 与基于格的密码学或 MPC-in-the-head 等技术的潜在联系

---

这是一个很好的想法！实现 **"Transparent SNARKs over Galois Rings"** 是一个有挑战性但非常有价值的项目。下面我为你提供一个详细的实现路线图：

## 🗺️ 实现路线图

### 第一阶段：理论准备与基础模块

#### 1. 深入理解论文
- 仔细阅读论文的每一节，特别关注：
  - Galois 环的定义与算术运算（$\mathbb{Z}_{p^k}[x]/(f(x))$）
  - 论文中使用的多项式承诺方案（Polynomial Commitment Scheme）
  - 算术化（Arithmetization）方法
  - FRI 协议或其他用于透明性的技术在环上的适配
  - 安全性证明中的关键引理

#### 2. 选择编程语言
推荐选项：

| 语言 | 优势 | 适用场景 |
|------|------|----------|
| **Rust** 🦀 | 高性能、内存安全、ZK 生态丰富（arkworks, plonky2） | 生产级实现 |
| **Python** 🐍 | 快速原型、数学库丰富（SageMath, SymPy） | 原型/验证 |
| **C++** | 极致性能、libsnark 等成熟库 | 高性能实现 |

**建议**：先用 **Python/SageMath** 做原型验证，再用 **Rust** 做正式实现。

---

### 第二阶段：核心模块实现

按以下顺序逐步构建：

#### 模块 1：Galois 环算术库
```
galois_ring/
├── ring.py          # Galois 环 Z_{p^k}[x]/(f(x)) 的定义
├── element.py       # 环元素的加、减、乘、（可逆元素的）逆运算
├── polynomial.py    # 环上多项式运算
├── ntt.py           # 环上的 NTT（数论变换）/ FFT
└── tests/           # 单元测试
```

关键实现点：
- 环 $\mathbb{Z}_{p^k}[x]/(f(x))$ 的模运算
- 处理**零因子**（zero divisors）—— 这是环与域的关键区别
- 高效的多项式乘法（NTT）

#### 模块 2：多项式承诺方案
```
commitment/
├── merkle_tree.py       # Merkle 树实现
├── hash.py              # 哈希函数（用于透明性）
├── fri.py               # FRI 协议（适配到 Galois 环）
├── poly_commitment.py   # 多项式承诺接口
└── tests/
```

#### 模块 3：算术化与约束系统
```
arithmetization/
├── r1cs.py              # R1CS 或论文特定的约束系统
├── circuit.py           # 算术电路表示
├── witness.py           # 见证生成
└── tests/
```

#### 模块 4：SNARK 协议核心
```
snark/
├── prover.py            # 证明者
├── verifier.py          # 验证者
├── transcript.py        # Fiat-Shamir 转换（非交互化）
├── params.py            # 公共参数
└── tests/
```

---

### 第三阶段：集成与测试

#### 1. 端到端测试
```python
# 伪代码示例
ring = GaloisRing(p=2, k=8, poly=irreducible_poly)
circuit = ArithmeticCircuit(ring)
circuit.add_constraint(...)

witness = circuit.generate_witness(inputs)
proof = Prover.prove(circuit, witness, public_input)
assert Verifier.verify(circuit, proof, public_input)
```

#### 2. 正确性验证
- 与已知的有限域上 SNARK 实现对比
- 使用论文中的测试向量（如果有）
- 边界情况：零因子、特殊输入

#### 3. 性能基准
- 证明生成时间 vs. 电路大小
- 证明大小
- 验证时间
- 与有限域 SNARK 的性能对比

---

### 第四阶段：优化与文档

- **性能优化**：NTT 加速、并行化、内存优化
- **文档**：API 文档、数学推导、使用示例
- **安全审计**：确保实现与论文安全证明一致

## Copilot

我已经成功读取了论文的内容。现在我对这篇论文有了全面的理解，下面为你做一个**完整的论文解析和代码实现指南**。

---

## 📄 论文内容总结

### 论文信息
- **标题**: Transparent SNARKs over Galois Rings
- **作者**: Yuanju Wei, Xinxuan Zhang, Yi Deng（中科院信息安全国家重点实验室）
- **关键词**: SNARKs · Galois rings · polynomial commitment

### 论文结构（5 大章节）

| 章节 | 内容 |
|------|------|
| **§1 Introduction** | 动机、贡献、技术概述 |
| **§2 Preliminaries** | Galois 环定义、SNARK 定义、多项式承诺方案定义 |
| **§3 Linear Codes over Galois Rings** | 扩展器码（Expander Codes）推广到 Galois 环 |
| **§4 Linear Time Polynomial Commitment** | Brakedown 多项式承诺方案推广到 Galois 环 |
| **§5 SNARKs over Galois Rings** | 结合 Libra/HyperPlonk 构建透明 SNARK |

### 核心贡献

1. **Expander Codes → Galois Rings**: 将 Brakedown 的扩展器码从有限域推广到任意 Galois 环 $\text{GR}(p^s, r)$，保持 $O(n)$ 编码时间
2. **Brakedown Polynomial Commitment → Galois Rings**: 基于上述线性码构建 Galois 环上的多项式承诺方案
3. **两个透明 SNARK 方案**:
   - **Libra + Brakedown**: 适用于 log-space uniform circuits，$O(n)$ 证明时间，$O(\sqrt{n})$ 证明大小
   - **HyperPlonk + Brakedown**: 适用于 NP circuits，$O(n\log^2 n)$ 证明时间，$O(\sqrt{n})$ 证明大小

### 核心技术难点

- **零因子问题**: Galois 环存在零因子，例如 $(x-1)(x-7) = (x-5)(x-3) \pmod{8}$，导致集合一致性检查无法直接从域推广到环
- **小环扩展**: 当 $p^r$ 不够大时，需要通过 $k$-fold 扩展将 $\text{GR}(p^s, r)$ 嵌入 $\text{GR}(p^s, kr)$
- **线性码检测引理**: 需要将 AHIV17 的检测引理推广到 Galois 环

---

## 🏗️ 基于你现有 Spartan 仓库的实现计划

你的仓库 `Entropy-pp/spartan-test` 已经是一个基于 Rust 的 Spartan SNARK 实现（使用 `curve25519-dalek`），有 sumcheck 协议、R1CS 等模块。我们可以在此基础上扩展。

### 推荐的实现模块划分

```
src/
├── galois_ring/           # 模块 1: Galois 环算术
│   ├── mod.rs
│   ├── element.rs         # GR(p^s, r) 元素运算
│   ├── polynomial.rs      # 环上多项式
│   └── extension.rs       # 小环扩展 GR(p^s,r) → GR(p^s,kr)
│
├── linear_code/           # 模块 2: Galois 环上的线性码 (§3)
│   ├── mod.rs
│   ├── expander.rs        # 扩展器码 (Algorithm 1)
│   ├── extended_enc.rs    # 小环编码 (Algorithm 2: Enc')
│   └── parameters.rs      # α, β, t, c_n, d_n 参数
│
├── poly_commitment_gr/    # 模块 3: Brakedown 多项式承诺 (§4)
│   ├── mod.rs
│   ├── commitment.rs      # Gen, Commit, Open, Eval
│   ├── verification.rs    # 线性码检测引理
│   └── merkle.rs          # Merkle 树承诺
│
├── snark_gr/              # 模块 4: Galois 环上的 SNARK (§5)
│   ├── mod.rs
│   ├── sumcheck_ring.rs   # 环上的 sumcheck 协议
│   ├── libra.rs           # Libra 框架 (log-space uniform)
│   └── hyperplonk.rs      # HyperPlonk 框架 (NP circuits)
│
├── lib.rs                 # 现有 Spartan 代码
├── sumcheck.rs            # 现有 sumcheck (可参考)
└── ...
```

### 按优先级的实现步骤

#### 步骤 1: Galois 环算术库（最基础）

关键数据结构：
```rust
// GR(p^s, r) = Z_{p^s}[x] / (f(x)), where f(x) is irreducible of degree r
pub struct GaloisRing {
    p: u64,           // 素数
    s: u32,           // p 的幂次
    r: u32,           // 不可约多项式的次数
    modulus: u64,     // p^s
    irred_poly: Vec<u64>,  // 不可约多项式 f(x) 的系数
}

pub struct GRElement {
    coeffs: Vec<u64>,  // 多项式系数 (长度 r)
    ring: Arc<GaloisRing>,
}

// 需要实现: Add, Sub, Mul, 可逆元素的 Inv
// 关键: 处理零因子 (d = gcd(a, p^s))
```

#### 步骤 2: 扩展器码（论文 §3, Algorithm 1 & 2）

```rust
// Algorithm 1: Enc: GR(p^s,r)^n → GR(p^s,r)^{tn}
pub fn encode(input: &[GRElement], params: &ExpanderParams) -> Vec<GRElement>;

// Algorithm 2: Enc': GR(p^s,r)^{kn} → GR(p^s,kr)^{tn} (小环扩展)
pub fn encode_extended(input: &[GRElement], k: usize, params: &ExpanderParams) -> Vec<GRElement>;
```

#### 步骤 3: Brakedown 多项式承诺（论文 §4）

```rust
pub trait PolyCommitmentGR {
    fn gen(security_param: usize, num_vars: usize) -> PublicParams;
    fn commit(pp: &PublicParams, poly: &MultilinearPoly, gamma: &[u8]) -> Commitment;
    fn open(pp: &PublicParams, commitment: &Commitment, poly: &MultilinearPoly, gamma: &[u8]) -> bool;
    fn eval(pp: &PublicParams, commitment: &Commitment, point: &[GRElement], value: &GRElement, poly: &MultilinearPoly) -> Proof;
}
```

#### 步骤 4: SNARK 协议（论文 §5）

结合你仓库中已有的 `sumcheck.rs` 进行修改，将 `Scalar`（curve25519）替换为 `GRElement`。

好的，我现在已经完全理解了论文的技术细节。下面给你一个**从零独立构建**的完整项目框架。

---

## 🏗️ 项目框架：Brakedown Polynomial Commitment over Galois Rings

### 项目名称建议：`brakedown-gr`

### 整体架构（自底向上 4 层依赖）

```
Layer 0 (底层)：Galois Ring 算术
Layer 1：线性码 (Expander Code over GR)
Layer 2：多项式承诺 (Brakedown PC over GR)
Layer 3：Transcript + 集成测试
```

### 目录结构

```
brakedown-gr/
├── Cargo.toml
├── README.md
│
├── src/
│   ├── lib.rs                      # 对外接口，re-export
│   │
│   │── ─── Layer 0: Galois Ring 算术 ───
│   ├── galois_ring/
│   │   ├── mod.rs                   # 模块入口
│   │   ├── ring.rs                  # GR(p^s, r) 结构体与参数
│   │   ├── element.rs               # 环元素：加/减/乘/gcd/可逆判断
│   │   ├── extension.rs             # 小环扩展：GR(p^s,r) → GR(p^s,kr)
│   │   ├── polynomial.rs            # 环上多项式运算
│   │   └── exceptional_set.rs       # 例外集(Exceptional Set)构造
│   │
│   │── ─── Layer 1: 线性码 ───
│   ├── linear_code/
│   │   ├── mod.rs
│   │   ├── parameters.rs            # α, β, t, c_n, d_n 参数计算
│   │   ├── sparse_matrix.rs         # 稀疏矩阵分布 M_{n,m,d}
│   │   ├── expander_code.rs         # Algorithm 1: Enc (大环编码)
│   │   ├── extended_code.rs         # Algorithm 2: Enc' (小环 → 扩展环编码)
│   │   └── distance.rs              # 码距分析 (Lemma 2, 3 的参数验证)
│   │
│   │── ─── Layer 2: 多项式承诺 ───
│   ├── poly_commit/
│   │   ├── mod.rs
│   │   ├── multilinear.rs           # 多线性多项式表示 + 求值
│   │   ├── matrix_layout.rs         # 系数矩阵 U = m×n 布局
│   │   ├── encoding.rs              # 对每行编码 → Û (编码后的系数矩阵)
│   │   ├── merkle.rs                # Merkle 树：对 Û 的列进行承诺
│   │   ├── testing.rs               # Testing Phase (AHIV17 重复引理)
│   │   ├── commitment.rs            # Commit Phase (Gen + Commit)
│   │   ├── evaluation.rs            # Eval Phase (Prover ↔ Verifier)
│   │   └── proof.rs                 # 证明结构体定义
│   │
│   │── ─── Layer 3: 基础设施 ───
│   ├── transcript.rs                # Fiat-Shamir transcript (挑战生成)
│   ├── hash.rs                      # 抗碰撞哈希函数 (SHA-256 / Blake3)
│   ├── errors.rs                    # 统一错误类型
│   └── utils.rs                     # 辅助函数
│
├── tests/
│   ├── test_galois_ring.rs          # 环算术正确性测试
│   ├── test_linear_code.rs          # 编码 + 码距测试
│   ├── test_poly_commit.rs          # 端到端: commit → eval → verify
│   └── test_small_ring.rs           # 小环扩展场景测试
│
├── benches/
│   ├── bench_encoding.rs            # 编码性能
│   └── bench_commitment.rs          # 承诺 + 验证性能
│
└── examples/
    └── simple_commit.rs             # 最简使用示例
```

---

### 各模块的详细职责与关键数据结构

#### Layer 0: `galois_ring/`

这是一切的地基，论文 §2.1 的内容。

```rust
// ====== ring.rs ======
/// GR(p^s, r) 的全局参数
pub struct GaloisRingParams {
    pub p: u64,                    // 素数
    pub s: u32,                    // 特征 p^s
    pub r: u32,                    // 不可约多项式次数
    pub modulus: u64,              // p^s
    pub irred_poly: Vec<u64>,      // f(x) ∈ Z[x], deg r, irreducible mod p
}

// ====== element.rs ======
/// GR(p^s, r) 中的元素 = a_0 + a_1*x + ... + a_{r-1}*x^{r-1}
pub struct GRElement {
    pub coeffs: Vec<u64>,          // 长度 r, 每个 ∈ [0, p^s)
}

impl GRElement {
    pub fn add(&self, other: &Self, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self;
    pub fn sub(&self, other: &Self, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self;
    pub fn mul(&self, other: &Self, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self;
    pub fn is_zero(&self) -> bool;
    pub fn is_unit(&self, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> bool;  // 是否可逆
    pub fn gcd_with_modulus(&self, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> u64; // Fact 2 中的 d
    pub fn inv(&self, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Option<Self>;     // 可逆时返回逆元
    pub fn random(rng: &mut impl Rng, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self;
    pub fn random_unit(rng: &mut impl Rng, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self; // 随机可逆元
}

// ====== extension.rs ======
/// 小环扩展: GR(p^s, r) → GR(p^s, kr)
/// 将 k 个 GR(p^s,r) 元素视为 GR(p^s,kr) 的一个元素 (Claim 1)
pub struct GaloisRingExtension {
    pub base_params: GaloisRingParams,    // GR(p^s, r)
    pub ext_params: GaloisRingParams,     // GR(p^s, kr)
    pub k: usize,
    pub ext_irred_poly: Vec<u64>,         // 扩展用的 k 次不可约多项式
}

impl GaloisRingExtension {
    pub fn pack(elements: &[GRElement]) -> GRElement;    // k 个小环元素 → 1 个大环元素
    pub fn unpack(ext_element: &GRElement) -> Vec<GRElement>; // 逆操作
}
```

#### Layer 1: `linear_code/`

论文 §3，将 Brakedown 的 expander code 推广到 Galois 环。

```rust
// ====== parameters.rs ======
/// Brakedown 编码参数 (Table 1)
pub struct ExpanderParams {
    pub alpha: f64,      // α ∈ (0,1)
    pub beta: f64,       // β ∈ (0,1)
    pub t: f64,          // t > (1+2β)/(1-α)
    pub c_n: usize,      // A 矩阵每行非零个数
    pub d_n: usize,      // B 矩阵每行非零个数
    pub n0: usize,       // 递归终止阈值
}

impl ExpanderParams {
    /// 根据 n 和 GR 参数自动选择最优参数组合
    pub fn from_ring(n: usize, ring: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self;
}

// ====== sparse_matrix.rs ======
/// M_{n,m,d}: 每行恰好 d 个非零项，从 GR 中随机选取
pub struct SparseMatrix {
    pub rows: usize,
    pub cols: usize,
    pub entries: Vec<Vec<(usize, GRElement)>>,  // (col_index, value)
}

impl SparseMatrix {
    pub fn random(rows: usize, cols: usize, d: usize, 
                  params: &GaloisRingParams, rng: &mut impl Rng) -> Self;
    pub fn mul_vec(&self, x: &[GRElement], params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Vec<GRElement>;
}

// ====== expander_code.rs ======
/// Algorithm 1: Enc: GR(p^s,r)^n → GR(p^s,r)^{tn}
pub struct ExpanderCode {
    pub params: ExpanderParams,
    pub ring_params: GaloisRingParams,
    pub matrices_a: Vec<SparseMatrix>,  // 各递归层的 A 矩阵
    pub matrices_b: Vec<SparseMatrix>,  // 各递归层的 B 矩阵
    pub base_matrix: Vec<Vec<GRElement>>, // n < n0 时的生成矩阵 M
}

impl ExpanderCode {
    pub fn setup(n: usize, ring: &GaloisRingParams, rng: &mut impl Rng) -> Self;
    pub fn encode(&self, x: &[GRElement]) -> Vec<GRElement>;  // 返回 w = (x, z, v)
    pub fn code_rate(&self) -> f64;
    pub fn code_distance(&self) -> usize;
}

// ====== extended_code.rs ======
/// Algorithm 2: Enc': GR(p^s,r)^{kn} → GR(p^s,kr)^{tn} (小环版本)
pub struct ExtendedExpanderCode {
    pub inner_code: ExpanderCode,       // 在 GR(p^s, kr) 上的 Enc
    pub extension: GaloisRingExtension, // GR(p^s,r) → GR(p^s,kr)
}

impl ExtendedExpanderCode {
    pub fn setup(n: usize, ring: &GaloisRingParams, rng: &mut impl Rng) -> Self;
    pub fn encode(&self, x: &[GRElement]) -> Vec<GRElement>;
}
```

#### Layer 2: `poly_commit/`

论文 §4，这是项目的**核心层**。

```rust
// ====== multilinear.rs ======
/// μ-变元多线性多项式 over GR(p^s, r)
/// 存储: 2^μ 个系数 (在超立方体 {0,1}^μ 上的求值)
pub struct MultilinearPoly {
    pub num_vars: usize,              // μ
    pub evals: Vec<GRElement>,        // 长度 2^μ
}

impl MultilinearPoly {
    pub fn evaluate(&self, point: &[GRElement], params: &GaloisRingParams) -> GRElement;
    pub fn to_matrix(&self) -> (Vec<Vec<GRElement>>, usize, usize);
    // 将 2^μ 个系数排成 2^{μ/2} × 2^{μ/2} 矩阵 U
}

// ====== matrix_layout.rs ======
/// 系数矩阵 U: m × n，其中 m = 2^{l/2}, n = 2^{l/2}
/// 以及编码后的矩阵 Û: m × (tn/k)
pub struct CoefficientMatrix {
    pub rows: Vec<Vec<GRElement>>,    // m 行, 每行 n 个元素
    pub m: usize,
    pub n: usize,
}

pub struct EncodedMatrix {
    pub rows: Vec<Vec<GRElement>>,    // m 行, 每行 tn/k 个 GR(p^s,kr) 元素
    pub m: usize,
    pub encoded_len: usize,           // tn/k (每行编码后长度，以扩展环元素计)
}

// ====== encoding.rs ======
/// 对系数矩阵的每一行进行编码
impl EncodedMatrix {
    pub fn from_coefficient_matrix(
        mat: &CoefficientMatrix,
        code: &ExtendedExpanderCode, // 或 ExpanderCode (大环情况)
    ) -> Self;
}

// ====== merkle.rs ======
/// Merkle 树承诺: 对 Û 的每一列做哈希承诺
pub struct MerkleTree {
    pub root: [u8; 32],
    nodes: Vec<[u8; 32]>,
    leaves: Vec<Vec<u8>>,
}

pub struct MerkleProof {
    pub path: Vec<[u8; 32]>,
    pub leaf_index: usize,
}

impl MerkleTree {
    pub fn build(columns: &[Vec<GRElement>]) -> Self;
    pub fn root(&self) -> [u8; 32];
    pub fn open(&self, index: usize) -> MerkleProof;
    pub fn verify(root: &[u8; 32], proof: &MerkleProof, leaf: &[u8]) -> bool;
}

// ====== commitment.rs ======
/// 公共参数
pub struct PublicParams {
    pub ring_params: GaloisRingParams,
    pub code: ExtendedExpanderCode,   // 线性码实例 (预处理的随机矩阵)
    pub security_param: usize,        // λ
    pub num_vars: usize,              // μ
    pub k: usize,                     // 扩展倍数 (大环时 k=1)
}

/// 承诺结果
pub struct Commitment {
    pub merkle_root: [u8; 32],        // Û 列的 Merkle 根
}

impl PublicParams {
    pub fn gen(security_param: usize, num_vars: usize, 
              ring_params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self;
}

pub fn commit(pp: &PublicParams, poly: &MultilinearPoly) -> (Commitment, CommitState);

/// 承诺时的私有状态 (Prover 保存，后续 Eval 用)
pub struct CommitState {
    pub coeff_matrix: CoefficientMatrix,   // U
    pub encoded_matrix: EncodedMatrix,     // Û
    pub merkle_tree: MerkleTree,
}

// ====== testing.rs ======
/// Testing Phase: AHIV17 重复引理 over GR
/// 论文 §4 核心: Verifier 通过多次从小环选挑战来保证 soundness
///
/// 协议:
///   1. V → P: 随机矩阵 R ∈ GR(p^s,r)^{k×m}
///   2. P → V: V_matrix = R * U ∈ GR(p^s,kr)^{k×(m/k)}, 声称 V=RU
///   3. V: 随机选 Q ⊂ [tm/k], |Q| = l_Q = Θ(λ)
///      对每个 j ∈ Q:
///        - 向 P 请求 Û 的第 j 列 + Merkle 路径
///        - 验证 Merkle 路径
///        - 验证 Enc(V_i)[j] = Σ_{s=1}^m R_i[s] · Û_s[j]

pub struct TestingProof {
    pub v_matrix: Vec<Vec<GRElement>>,       // k × (m/k) 的 V 矩阵
    pub queried_columns: Vec<QueriedColumn>,  // 每个 j ∈ Q 的列数据
}

pub struct QueriedColumn {
    pub index: usize,
    pub column: Vec<GRElement>,               // Û 的第 j 列 (m 个元素)
    pub merkle_proof: MerkleProof,
}

// ====== evaluation.rs ======
/// Eval Phase: Prover 证明 f(z) = v
///
/// 协议:
///   1. V 计算 q1 和 q2 向量 (基于求值点 z)
///      q1 = (1-r1, r1) ⊗ ... ⊗ (1-r_{l/2}, r_{l/2})
///      q2 = (1-r_{l/2+1}, r_{l/2+1}) ⊗ ... ⊗ (1-r_l, r_l)
///   2. P 计算 w = q1^T * Û (线性组合编码行)
///   3. V 验证 w 是合法码字 (Testing Phase)
///   4. V 通过解码 w 得到 q1^T * U, 然后与 q2 做内积验证 f(z) = v

pub struct EvalProof {
    pub w: Vec<GRElement>,           // q1^T * Û (编码行的线性组合)
    pub testing_proof: TestingProof, // Testing Phase 的证明
}

pub fn eval_prove(
    pp: &PublicParams,
    commitment: &Commitment,
    state: &CommitState,
    point: &[GRElement],         // z ∈ GR(p^s,r)^μ
    value: &GRElement,           // v = f(z)
    transcript: &mut Transcript,
) -> EvalProof;

pub fn eval_verify(
    pp: &PublicParams,
    commitment: &Commitment,
    point: &[GRElement],
    value: &GRElement,
    proof: &EvalProof,
    transcript: &mut Transcript,
) -> Result<(), VerifyError>;

// ====== proof.rs ======
/// 统一的证明结构 (可序列化)
pub struct BrakedownProof {
    pub commitment: Commitment,
    pub eval_proof: EvalProof,
}
```

#### Layer 3: 基础设施

```rust
// ====== transcript.rs ======
/// Fiat-Shamir Transcript: 将交互式协议转为非交互式
pub struct Transcript {
    state: Vec<u8>,  // 内部用 hash chain
}

impl Transcript {
    pub fn new(label: &[u8]) -> Self;
    pub fn append_message(&mut self, label: &[u8], msg: &[u8]);
    pub fn append_gr_element(&mut self, label: &[u8], elem: &GRElement);
    pub fn challenge_gr_element(&mut self, label: &[u8], params: &GaloisRingParams) -> GRElement;
    pub fn challenge_gr_matrix(&mut self, label: &[u8], rows: usize, cols: usize, 
                                params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Vec<Vec<GRElement>>;
    pub fn challenge_index_set(&mut self, label: &[u8], size: usize, domain: usize) -> Vec<usize>;
}

// ====== hash.rs ======
pub fn hash_column(column: &[GRElement]) -> [u8; 32];
pub fn hash_combine(left: &[u8; 32], right: &[u8; 32]) -> [u8; 32];
```

---

### 实现优先级路线图

```
Phase 1 (Week 1-2): Galois Ring 算术
  ├── GR(p^s, r) 元素的加减乘
  ├── gcd / 可逆判断 / 求逆 (Fact 2)
  ├── 随机元素采样
  └── 单元测试 (对比 SageMath)

Phase 2 (Week 2-3): Expander Code
  ├── 参数计算 (Table 1)
  ├── 稀疏矩阵采样 + 矩阵向量乘
  ├── Algorithm 1: 大环编码 Enc
  ├── Algorithm 2: 小环扩展编码 Enc'
  └── 编码正确性测试 (线性性验证)

Phase 3 (Week 3-5): Polynomial Commitment
  ├── 多线性多项式 → 系数矩阵 U
  ├── 逐行编码 → Û + Merkle 树
  ├── Testing Phase (重复引理)
  ├── Commit + Eval + Verify 完整流程
  └── 端到端测试

Phase 4 (Week 5-6): 优化 + 打磨
  ├── Fiat-Shamir 非交互化
  ├── 序列化 / 证明大小优化
  ├── Benchmark
  └── 文档 + Examples
```

---

### 关键依赖 (`Cargo.toml`)

```toml
[package]
name = "brakedown-gr"
version = "0.1.0"
edition = "2021"

[dependencies]
rand = "0.8"
sha2 = "0.10"          # 或 blake3 = "1.5"
serde = { version = "1", features = ["derive"] }
bincode = "1"

[dev-dependencies]
criterion = "0.5"

[[bench]]
name = "bench_commitment"
harness = false
```

依赖非常轻量——论文方案的最大优点就是**只依赖抗碰撞哈希函数**，不需要椭圆曲线/配对等重密码学原语。

---

### 一个注意点

论文区分了两种情况，你在实现时需要覆盖：

| 情况 | 条件 | 编码方式 | k 值 |
|------|------|----------|------|
| **大环** | $p^r \geq 2^{127}$ | 直接用 Algorithm 1 (Enc) | k = 1 |
| **小环** | $p^r < 2^{127}$ | 先扩展再编码 Algorithm 2 (Enc') | k ≥ 2, 使得 $p^{kr} \geq 2^{127}$ |

Testing Phase 也因此不同：大环时 Verifier 从大环选挑战直接验；小环时用"重复版引理"，从小环多次选挑战。

## Copilot

现在我把论文 §2.1 中关于 Galois 环的所有数学定义和事实都精确地提取出来了。下面是完整的实现。

---

两个文件之间的数学关系：

- `ring.rs` 定义 $\text{GR}(p^s, r) \cong \mathbb{Z}[x]/(p^s, f(x))$ 的**全局参数**，包括不可约多项式的查找
- `element.rs` 定义环中元素 $a_0 + a_1 x + \cdots + a_{r-1} x^{r-1}$ 的**算术运算**，包括 Fact 2 中的 $\gcd(a, p^s)$ 和求逆

```rust name=src/galois_ring/ring.rs
//! Galois Ring GR(p^s, r) global parameters.
//!
//! A Galois ring is defined as:
//!     GR(p^s, r) ≅ Z[x] / (p^s, f(x))
//! where f(x) ∈ Z[x] is a monic polynomial of degree r, irreducible mod p.
//!
//! The ring has p^{sr} elements total. Its unique maximal ideal is (p),
//! and all zero divisors lie in (p) (Fact 1).

use std::fmt;

/// Parameters defining a Galois ring GR(p^s, r).
///
/// - `p`: a prime number
/// - `s`: the characteristic exponent (characteristic = p^s)
/// - `r`: the degree of the irreducible polynomial f(x)
/// - `modulus`: p^s (all coefficient arithmetic is mod p^s)
/// - `irred_poly`: coefficients of f(x) = x^r + c_{r-1}*x^{r-1} + ... + c_0,
///   stored as [c_0, c_1, ..., c_{r-1}]. The leading coefficient 1 is implicit.
#[derive(Clone, Debug)]
pub struct GaloisRingParams {
    pub p: u64,
    pub s: u32,
    pub r: u32,
    pub modulus: u64, // p^s
    pub irred_poly: Vec<u64>, // length r, coefficients mod p^s (leading x^r is implicit)
}

impl GaloisRingParams {
    /// Construct GR(p^s, r) with an explicit irreducible polynomial.
    ///
    /// `irred_coeffs` should be the coefficients [c_0, c_1, ..., c_{r-1}]
    /// of f(x) = x^r + c_{r-1}*x^{r-1} + ... + c_0.
    ///
    /// # Panics
    /// Panics if p is not prime, s == 0, r == 0, or the polynomial length is wrong.
    pub fn new(p: u64, s: u32, r: u32, irred_coeffs: Vec<u64>) -> Self {
        assert!(s > 0, "s must be positive");
        assert!(r > 0, "r must be positive");
        assert!(is_prime(p), "p must be prime");
        assert_eq!(
            irred_coeffs.len(),
            r as usize,
            "irred_coeffs must have exactly r elements"
        );

        let modulus = checked_pow(p, s);

        // Normalize coefficients mod p^s
        let irred_poly: Vec<u64> = irred_coeffs.iter().map(|&c| c % modulus).collect();

        let params = GaloisRingParams {
            p,
            s,
            r,
            modulus,
            irred_poly,
        };

        // Verify irreducibility mod p
        debug_assert!(
            params.is_irred_mod_p(),
            "f(x) must be irreducible mod p"
        );

        params
    }

    /// Construct GR(p^s, r) by automatically finding an irreducible polynomial
    /// of degree r over GF(p), then lifting it to Z_{p^s}[x].
    ///
    /// Uses brute-force search among monic polynomials of degree r over GF(p).
    /// This is fine for small p and r (which is the typical case).
    pub fn new_auto(p: u64, s: u32, r: u32) -> Self {
        assert!(s > 0 && r > 0);
        assert!(is_prime(p));

        if r == 1 {
            // x + 0 is trivially irreducible (any degree-1 monic poly works)
            // But we want f(x) = x, so the quotient ring is Z_{p^s} itself.
            // Actually for r=1, GR(p^s, 1) = Z_{p^s}, we can use f(x) = x.
            // The element is just a_0, and x ≡ 0, so this is correct.
            // But more standardly, if r=1 we simply use GR(p^s, 1) ≅ Z_{p^s}.
            let modulus = checked_pow(p, s);
            return GaloisRingParams {
                p,
                s,
                r: 1,
                modulus,
                irred_poly: vec![0], // f(x) = x, so c_0 = 0
            };
        }

        let modulus = checked_pow(p, s);

        // Search for an irreducible polynomial of degree r over GF(p).
        // We enumerate monic polynomials f(x) = x^r + c_{r-1}*x^{r-1} + ... + c_0
        // with coefficients in {0, ..., p-1} and check irreducibility over GF(p).
        let coeffs = find_irreducible_poly(p, r);

        GaloisRingParams {
            p,
            s,
            r,
            modulus,
            irred_poly: coeffs,
        }
    }

    /// Total number of elements in the ring: p^{sr}
    pub fn order(&self) -> u128 {
        (self.p as u128).pow(self.s * self.r)
    }

    /// Number of units (invertible elements): p^{sr} - p^{(s-1)r}
    /// (elements not in the maximal ideal (p))
    pub fn num_units(&self) -> u128 {
        let total = self.order();
        let ideal_size = (self.p as u128).pow((self.s - 1) * self.r);
        // Elements in (p) are of the form p * a where a ∈ GR(p^s, r),
        // but more precisely |(p)| = p^{(s-1)r}.
        total - ideal_size
    }

    /// Whether p^r is large enough for direct encoding (no extension needed).
    /// Per the paper, we need p^r >= 2^127 for the large-ring case.
    pub fn is_large_ring(&self, security_bits: u32) -> bool {
        // Check if p^r >= 2^security_bits
        // Use logarithms to avoid overflow
        let log2_pr = (self.r as f64) * (self.p as f64).log2();
        log2_pr >= security_bits as f64
    }

    /// Compute the extension factor k needed to make the ring "large".
    /// We need p^{kr} >= 2^security_bits, so k >= ceil(security_bits / (r * log2(p))).
    pub fn extension_degree(&self, security_bits: u32) -> usize {
        if self.is_large_ring(security_bits) {
            return 1;
        }
        let log2_pr = (self.r as f64) * (self.p as f64).log2();
        let k = ((security_bits as f64) / log2_pr).ceil() as usize;
        k.max(1)
    }

    /// Check if the stored polynomial is irreducible mod p.
    fn is_irred_mod_p(&self) -> bool {
        // Build the full polynomial mod p: [c_0, c_1, ..., c_{r-1}, 1]
        let mut poly_mod_p: Vec<u64> = self.irred_poly.iter().map(|&c| c % self.p).collect();
        poly_mod_p.push(1); // leading coefficient
        is_irreducible_mod_p(&poly_mod_p, self.p)
    }
}

impl fmt::Display for GaloisRingParams {
    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {
        write!(
            f,
            "GR({}^{}, {}) [modulus={}, f(x)=x^{}",
            self.p, self.s, self.r, self.modulus, self.r
        )?;
        for i in (0..self.r as usize).rev() {
            let c = self.irred_poly[i];
            if c != 0 {
                write!(f, " + {}*x^{}", c, i)?;
            }
        }
        write!(f, "]")
    }
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
//  Utility functions
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

/// Compute base^exp as u64 with overflow check.
fn checked_pow(base: u64, exp: u32) -> u64 {
    base.checked_pow(exp).expect("p^s overflows u64")
}

/// Simple primality test (trial division), sufficient for small primes.
fn is_prime(n: u64) -> bool {
    if n < 2 {
        return false;
    }
    if n == 2 || n == 3 {
        return true;
    }
    if n % 2 == 0 || n % 3 == 0 {
        return false;
    }
    let mut i = 5u64;
    while i * i <= n {
        if n % i == 0 || n % (i + 2) == 0 {
            return false;
        }
        i += 6;
    }
    true
}

/// Polynomial arithmetic mod p (coefficients in GF(p)).
/// Polynomials are stored as Vec<u64> with index = degree.

/// Multiply two polynomials mod p.
fn poly_mul_mod_p(a: &[u64], b: &[u64], p: u64) -> Vec<u64> {
    if a.is_empty() || b.is_empty() {
        return vec![];
    }
    let mut result = vec![0u64; a.len() + b.len() - 1];
    for (i, &ai) in a.iter().enumerate() {
        for (j, &bj) in b.iter().enumerate() {
            result[i + j] = (result[i + j] + ai as u128 * bj as u128 % p as u128) as u64 % p;
        }
    }
    result
}

/// Compute polynomial mod (divisor) over GF(p). Returns the remainder.
fn poly_rem_mod_p(num: &[u64], den: &[u64], p: u64) -> Vec<u64> {
    assert!(!den.is_empty() && *den.last().unwrap() != 0);
    let mut rem: Vec<u64> = num.to_vec();
    let den_deg = den.len() - 1;
    let den_lead_inv = mod_inv(den[den_deg], p).expect("leading coeff must be invertible mod p");

    while rem.len() > den.len() || (rem.len() == den.len() && rem.len() > 1) {
        let rem_deg = rem.len() - 1;
        if rem_deg < den_deg {
            break;
        }
        let coeff = (rem[rem_deg] as u128 * den_lead_inv as u128 % p as u128) as u64;
        if coeff == 0 {
            rem.pop();
            continue;
        }
        let shift = rem_deg - den_deg;
        for (i, &d) in den.iter().enumerate() {
            let sub = (coeff as u128 * d as u128 % p as u128) as u64;
            rem[shift + i] = (rem[shift + i] + p - sub) % p;
        }
        // Remove leading zeros
        while rem.len() > 1 && *rem.last().unwrap() == 0 {
            rem.pop();
        }
    }
    rem
}

/// Modular inverse of a mod p (p is prime) via Fermat's little theorem.
fn mod_inv(a: u64, p: u64) -> Option<u64> {
    let a = a % p;
    if a == 0 {
        return None;
    }
    Some(mod_pow(a, p - 2, p))
}

/// Modular exponentiation: base^exp mod modulus.
fn mod_pow(mut base: u64, mut exp: u64, modulus: u64) -> u64 {
    if modulus == 1 {
        return 0;
    }
    let mut result = 1u128;
    base %= modulus;
    let m = modulus as u128;
    let mut b = base as u128;
    while exp > 0 {
        if exp & 1 == 1 {
            result = result * b % m;
        }
        exp >>= 1;
        b = b * b % m;
    }
    result as u64
}

/// Check if a polynomial (with explicit leading coefficient) is irreducible over GF(p).
///
/// Uses the standard algorithm: f is irreducible of degree r over GF(p) iff:
///   1. x^{p^r} ≡ x (mod f) over GF(p)
///   2. gcd(x^{p^i} - x, f) = 1 for all 1 <= i < r
fn is_irreducible_mod_p(poly: &[u64], p: u64) -> bool {
    let deg = poly.len() - 1;
    if deg == 0 {
        return false;
    }
    if deg == 1 {
        return true; // degree 1 is always irreducible
    }

    // We need to compute x^{p^i} mod f(x) over GF(p) for i = 1..r.
    // Start with h = x, then repeatedly compute h = h^p mod f.
    let x_poly = vec![0u64, 1]; // the polynomial "x"

    let mut h = poly_pow_mod(& x_poly, p, poly, p);

    for i in 1..=deg {
        // h = x^{p^i} mod f at this point
        // Check gcd(h - x, f) for i < deg
        let mut h_minus_x = h.clone();
        // Subtract x: h_minus_x[1] -= 1
        if h_minus_x.len() < 2 {
            h_minus_x.resize(2, 0);
        }
        h_minus_x[1] = (h_minus_x[1] + p - 1) % p;

        if i < deg {
            let g = poly_gcd_mod_p(&h_minus_x, poly, p);
            // gcd should be 1 (constant) for irreducibility
            if g.len() != 1 || g[0] != 1 {
                // Normalize: gcd might be [c] for some c != 1 — that's still degree 0
                let is_const = g.len() == 1 || (g.len() > 1 && g.iter().skip(1).all(|&c| c == 0));
                if !is_const {
                    return false;
                }
            }
        } else {
            // i == deg: check x^{p^r} ≡ x (mod f), i.e. h_minus_x ≡ 0
            let all_zero = h_minus_x.iter().all(|&c| c % p == 0);
            if !all_zero {
                return false;
            }
        }

        if i < deg {
            // h <- h^p mod f for next iteration
            h = poly_pow_mod(&h, p, poly, p);
        }
    }
    true
}

/// Compute poly^exp mod modpoly, all arithmetic mod p.
fn poly_pow_mod(poly: &[u64], exp: u64, modpoly: &[u64], p: u64) -> Vec<u64> {
    let mut result = vec![1u64]; // polynomial "1"
    let mut base = poly_rem_mod_p(poly, modpoly, p);
    let mut e = exp;

    while e > 0 {
        if e & 1 == 1 {
            result = poly_mul_mod_p(&result, &base, p);
            result = poly_rem_mod_p(&result, modpoly, p);
        }
        e >>= 1;
        if e > 0 {
            let tmp = poly_mul_mod_p(&base, &base, p);
            base = poly_rem_mod_p(&tmp, modpoly, p);
        }
    }
    result
}

/// GCD of two polynomials over GF(p).
fn poly_gcd_mod_p(a: &[u64], b: &[u64], p: u64) -> Vec<u64> {
    let mut a = a.to_vec();
    let mut b = b.to_vec();
    // Remove leading zeros
    while a.len() > 1 && *a.last().unwrap() == 0 {
        a.pop();
    }
    while b.len() > 1 && *b.last().unwrap() == 0 {
        b.pop();
    }

    while b.len() > 1 || (b.len() == 1 && b[0] != 0) {
        let r = poly_rem_mod_p(&a, &b, p);
        a = b;
        b = r;
        while b.len() > 1 && *b.last().unwrap() == 0 {
            b.pop();
        }
    }
    // Make monic
    if !a.is_empty() && *a.last().unwrap() != 0 {
        let lead_inv = mod_inv(*a.last().unwrap(), p).unwrap_or(1);
        for c in a.iter_mut() {
            *c = (*c as u128 * lead_inv as u128 % p as u128) as u64;
        }
    }
    a
}

/// Find an irreducible monic polynomial of degree r over GF(p).
/// Returns coefficients [c_0, c_1, ..., c_{r-1}] (the leading x^r is implicit).
///
/// Uses brute-force enumeration. For small p and r this is perfectly fine.
fn find_irreducible_poly(p: u64, r: u32) -> Vec<u64> {
    let r = r as usize;
    // Enumerate all monic polynomials of degree r: x^r + c_{r-1}*x^{r-1} + ... + c_0
    let mut coeffs = vec![0u64; r]; // [c_0, ..., c_{r-1}]

    loop {
        // Build full polynomial for testing: [c_0, ..., c_{r-1}, 1]
        let mut full = coeffs.clone();
        full.push(1);

        if is_irreducible_mod_p(&full, p) {
            return coeffs;
        }

        // Increment coefficients (mixed radix counter base p)
        let mut carry = true;
        for c in coeffs.iter_mut() {
            if carry {
                *c += 1;
                if *c >= p {
                    *c = 0;
                    carry = true;
                } else {
                    carry = false;
                }
            }
        }
        if carry {
            panic!(
                "No irreducible polynomial of degree {} found over GF({}). This should not happen.",
                r, p
            );
        }
    }
}

// Re-export utility for element.rs
pub(crate) fn mod_pow_u64(base: u64, exp: u64, modulus: u64) -> u64 {
    mod_pow(base, exp, modulus)
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn test_is_prime() {
        assert!(!is_prime(0));
        assert!(!is_prime(1));
        assert!(is_prime(2));
        assert!(is_prime(3));
        assert!(!is_prime(4));
        assert!(is_prime(5));
        assert!(is_prime(127));
        assert!(!is_prime(128));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_gr_z4() {
        // GR(2^2, 1) = Z_4, f(x) = x
        let params = GaloisRingParams::new(2, 2, 1, vec![0]);
        assert_eq!(params.modulus, 4);
        assert_eq!(params.order(), 4);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_auto_gf4_extension() {
        // GR(2, 2) ≅ GF(4), should find x^2 + x + 1 (irreducible over GF(2))
        let params = GaloisRingParams::new_auto(2, 1, 2);
        assert_eq!(params.r, 2);
        assert_eq!(params.modulus, 2);
        // x^2 + x + 1 has coeffs [1, 1] (c_0=1, c_1=1)
        assert_eq!(params.irred_poly, vec![1, 1]);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_auto_gr_p2_r2() {
        // GR(4, 2): Z_4[x]/(f(x)) where f is irreducible of degree 2 mod 2
        let params = GaloisRingParams::new_auto(2, 2, 2);
        assert_eq!(params.modulus, 4);
        assert_eq!(params.r, 2);
        assert_eq!(params.order(), 16); // 2^{2*2} = 16
        // f(x) should be x^2 + x + 1 lifted to Z_4
        assert_eq!(params.irred_poly, vec![1, 1]);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_auto_gf8() {
        // GR(2, 3) ≅ GF(8), irreducible degree 3 over GF(2)
        let params = GaloisRingParams::new_auto(2, 1, 3);
        assert_eq!(params.r, 3);
        // x^3 + x + 1 is the first irreducible: coeffs [1, 1, 0]
        assert_eq!(params.irred_poly, vec![1, 1, 0]);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_auto_gf_p3_r2() {
        // GR(3, 2) over GF(3), degree 2
        let params = GaloisRingParams::new_auto(3, 1, 2);
        assert_eq!(params.r, 2);
        // x^2 + 1 is irreducible over GF(3) (no roots: 0^2+1=1, 1^2+1=2, 2^2+1=2)
        // Or x^2 + x + 2 might come first depending on enumeration order.
        // Our enumeration starts from [0,0] and increments c_0 first.
        // [1, 0] -> x^2 + 1 -> check: roots mod 3: 0->1, 1->2, 2->2. No root, degree 2 => irreducible.
        assert_eq!(params.irred_poly, vec![1, 0]);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_large_ring_check() {
        // GR(2, 128): 2^128 >= 2^127 → large
        let params = GaloisRingParams::new_auto(2, 1, 2);
        assert!(!params.is_large_ring(127)); // 2^2 = 4, not large
        assert_eq!(params.extension_degree(127), 64); // need k=64 so 2^{64*2}=2^128 >= 2^127
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_poly_irreducibility() {
        // x^2 + x + 1 over GF(2): irreducible
        assert!(is_irreducible_mod_p(&[1, 1, 1], 2));
        // x^2 + 1 over GF(2): reducible (= (x+1)^2)
        assert!(!is_irreducible_mod_p(&[1, 0, 1], 2));
        // x^2 + 1 over GF(3): irreducible
        assert!(is_irreducible_mod_p(&[1, 0, 1], 3));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_display() {
        let params = GaloisRingParams::new_auto(2, 2, 2);
        let s = format!("{}", params);
        assert!(s.contains("GR(2^2, 2)"));
    }
}
```

```rust name=src/galois_ring/element.rs
//! Elements of a Galois ring GR(p^s, r).
//!
//! An element is a polynomial a_0 + a_1*x + ... + a_{r-1}*x^{r-1}
//! with coefficients in Z_{p^s}, modulo the irreducible polynomial f(x).
//!
//! Key facts from the paper:
//! - Fact 1: All zero divisors are in the ideal (p).
//! - Fact 2: If gcd(a, p^s) = d, the equation ax = b has at most d^r solutions.
//!           In particular, a is a unit iff gcd(a, p^s) = 1.
//! - Definition 2: gcd(a, n) = gcd(a_0, ..., a_{r-1}, n).

use super::ring::GaloisRingParams;
use rand::Rng;
use std::fmt;

/// An element of GR(p^s, r), represented as a polynomial of degree < r
/// with coefficients in Z_{p^s}.
#[derive(Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]
pub struct GRElement {
    /// Coefficients [a_0, a_1, ..., a_{r-1}], each in [0, p^s).
    pub coeffs: Vec<u64>,
}

impl GRElement {
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------
    //  Constructors
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------

    /// Create an element from raw coefficients.
    /// The length must equal params.r, and each coefficient must be < params.modulus.
    pub fn new(coeffs: Vec<u64>, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self {
        assert_eq!(coeffs.len(), params.r as usize);
        let coeffs = coeffs.iter().map(|&c| c % params.modulus).collect();
        GRElement { coeffs }
    }

    /// The zero element.
    pub fn zero(params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self {
        GRElement {
            coeffs: vec![0u64; params.r as usize],
        }
    }

    /// The one element (multiplicative identity).
    pub fn one(params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self {
        let mut coeffs = vec![0u64; params.r as usize];
        coeffs[0] = 1;
        GRElement { coeffs }
    }

    /// Create an element from a single integer (constant polynomial).
    pub fn from_int(val: u64, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self {
        let mut coeffs = vec![0u64; params.r as usize];
        coeffs[0] = val % params.modulus;
        GRElement { coeffs }
    }

    /// Sample a uniformly random element from GR(p^s, r).
    pub fn random(rng: &mut impl Rng, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self {
        let coeffs: Vec<u64> = (0..params.r)
            .map(|_| rng.gen_range(0..params.modulus))
            .collect();
        GRElement { coeffs }
    }

    /// Sample a uniformly random unit (invertible element).
    /// An element is a unit iff gcd(a, p^s) = 1,
    /// i.e., at least one coefficient is coprime to p.
    pub fn random_unit(rng: &mut impl Rng, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self {
        loop {
            let elem = Self::random(rng, params);
            if elem.is_unit(params) {
                return elem;
            }
        }
    }

    /// Sample a uniformly random non-zero element.
    pub fn random_nonzero(rng: &mut impl Rng, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self {
        loop {
            let elem = Self::random(rng, params);
            if !elem.is_zero() {
                return elem;
            }
        }
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------
    //  Predicates
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------

    /// Check if this element is zero.
    pub fn is_zero(&self) -> bool {
        self.coeffs.iter().all(|&c| c == 0)
    }

    /// Check if this element is a unit (invertible).
    ///
    /// By Fact 1, an element is a unit iff it is NOT in the ideal (p),
    /// which happens iff gcd(a_0, ..., a_{r-1}, p^s) = 1,
    /// equivalently, iff at least one a_i is coprime to p.
    pub fn is_unit(&self, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> bool {
        self.gcd_with_modulus(params) == 1
    }

    /// Check if this element is a zero divisor.
    ///
    /// By Fact 1: all zero divisors lie in the ideal (p).
    /// The zero element is technically a zero divisor, but we also return true
    /// for non-zero elements in (p).
    pub fn is_zero_divisor(&self, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> bool {
        !self.is_zero() && !self.is_unit(params)
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------
    //  Core arithmetic: Add, Sub, Neg
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------

    /// Addition in GR(p^s, r): component-wise mod p^s.
    pub fn add(&self, other: &Self, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self {
        debug_assert_eq!(self.coeffs.len(), other.coeffs.len());
        let coeffs = self
            .coeffs
            .iter()
            .zip(other.coeffs.iter())
            .map(|(&a, &b)| (a + b) % params.modulus)
            .collect();
        GRElement { coeffs }
    }

    /// Subtraction in GR(p^s, r): component-wise mod p^s.
    pub fn sub(&self, other: &Self, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self {
        debug_assert_eq!(self.coeffs.len(), other.coeffs.len());
        let coeffs = self
            .coeffs
            .iter()
            .zip(other.coeffs.iter())
            .map(|(&a, &b)| (a + params.modulus - b) % params.modulus)
            .collect();
        GRElement { coeffs }
    }

    /// Additive inverse (negation).
    pub fn neg(&self, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self {
        let coeffs = self
            .coeffs
            .iter()
            .map(|&a| if a == 0 { 0 } else { params.modulus - a })
            .collect();
        GRElement { coeffs }
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------
    //  Core arithmetic: Multiplication
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------

    /// Multiplication in GR(p^s, r).
    ///
    /// Step 1: Polynomial multiplication of the two elements (schoolbook).
    /// Step 2: Reduce modulo f(x), with all coefficient arithmetic mod p^s.
    pub fn mul(&self, other: &Self, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self {
        let r = params.r as usize;
        let m = params.modulus as u128;

        // Step 1: polynomial multiplication → degree up to 2(r-1)
        let mut product = vec![0u128; 2 * r - 1];
        for (i, &ai) in self.coeffs.iter().enumerate() {
            for (j, &bj) in other.coeffs.iter().enumerate() {
                product[i + j] = (product[i + j] + ai as u128 * bj as u128) % m;
            }
        }

        // Step 2: reduce mod f(x) = x^r + c_{r-1}*x^{r-1} + ... + c_0
        // Process from the highest degree down to r.
        // When we encounter a term c * x^k with k >= r, replace it with
        // -c * (c_0 + c_1*x + ... + c_{r-1}*x^{r-1}), since x^r ≡ -(c_0 + ... + c_{r-1}*x^{r-1}).
        for k in (r..product.len()).rev() {
            let coeff = product[k];
            if coeff == 0 {
                continue;
            }
            product[k] = 0;
            for (i, &fi) in params.irred_poly.iter().enumerate() {
                // Subtract coeff * f_i from position k - r + i
                let pos = k - r + i;
                product[pos] = (product[pos] + m - (coeff * fi as u128 % m)) % m;
            }
        }

        let coeffs = product[..r].iter().map(|&c| c as u64).collect();
        GRElement { coeffs }
    }

    /// Scalar multiplication: multiply by an integer in Z_{p^s}.
    pub fn scalar_mul(&self, scalar: u64, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self {
        let m = params.modulus as u128;
        let s = scalar as u128;
        let coeffs = self
            .coeffs
            .iter()
            .map(|&a| (a as u128 * s % m) as u64)
            .collect();
        GRElement { coeffs }
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------
    //  GCD and invertibility (Fact 2, Definition 2)
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------

    /// Compute gcd(a, p^s) as defined in Definition 2 of the paper:
    ///   gcd(a, p^s) = gcd(a_0, a_1, ..., a_{r-1}, p^s)
    ///
    /// This value determines:
    /// - Whether the element is a unit (gcd = 1)
    /// - The number of solutions to ax = b (at most d^r, by Fact 2)
    /// - The "class" of zero divisor for the code distance analysis
    pub fn gcd_with_modulus(&self, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> u64 {
        let mut g = params.modulus;
        for &c in &self.coeffs {
            g = gcd_u64(g, c);
            if g == 1 {
                return 1;
            }
        }
        g
    }

    /// Determine which ideal class this element belongs to.
    ///
    /// Returns the largest i such that this element is in the ideal (p^i).
    /// - Returns s if the element is zero.
    /// - Returns 0 if the element is a unit.
    ///
    /// This is used in the code distance analysis (§3.1) where zero divisors
    /// are classified by their ideal membership.
    pub fn ideal_class(&self, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> u32 {
        if self.is_zero() {
            return params.s;
        }
        let d = self.gcd_with_modulus(params);
        // d divides p^s, so d = p^i for some i.
        // Find the largest i such that p^i divides d.
        let mut i = 0u32;
        let mut power = 1u64;
        while i < params.s {
            power *= params.p;
            if d % power != 0 {
                break;
            }
            i += 1;
        }
        i
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------
    //  Inversion
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------

    /// Compute the multiplicative inverse, if it exists.
    ///
    /// An element is invertible iff gcd(a, p^s) = 1 (i.e., it's a unit).
    ///
    /// Algorithm: lift to Z_{p^s}[x]/(f(x)) and use extended Euclidean algorithm
    /// on polynomials, or use the iterative Newton lifting approach:
    ///   1. Find inverse mod p (in GF(p^r) = GR(p^1, r))
    ///   2. Hensel-lift: for i = 1..s-1, a^{-1} mod p^{2^i}
    ///
    /// We use the simpler approach of the extended polynomial GCD over Z_{p^s}[x].
    /// For practical ring sizes this is efficient enough.
    pub fn inv(&self, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Option<Self> {
        if !self.is_unit(params) {
            return None;
        }

        if params.s == 1 {
            // GR(p, r) = GF(p^r): use Fermat's theorem.
            // a^{-1} = a^{p^r - 2} in GF(p^r).
            return Some(self.pow_in_field(params));
        }

        // General case: Hensel lifting.
        // Step 1: Compute inverse mod p (in GF(p^r)).
        let gf_params = GaloisRingParams {
            p: params.p,
            s: 1,
            r: params.r,
            modulus: params.p,
            irred_poly: params.irred_poly.iter().map(|&c| c % params.p).collect(),
        };
        let a_mod_p = self.reduce_mod(&gf_params);
        let inv_mod_p = a_mod_p.pow_in_field(&gf_params);

        // Step 2: Hensel lift from mod p to mod p^s.
        // Newton's method: if a * x ≡ 1 (mod p^k), then
        //   x' = x * (2 - a*x) satisfies a * x' ≡ 1 (mod p^{2k})
        let mut current_inv = inv_mod_p;
        let mut current_mod = params.p;

        while current_mod < params.modulus {
            let next_mod = std::cmp::min(
                (current_mod as u128 * current_mod as u128) as u64,
                params.modulus,
            );
            let lift_params = GaloisRingParams {
                p: params.p,
                s: params.s, // we'll manually work mod next_mod
                r: params.r,
                modulus: next_mod,
                irred_poly: params.irred_poly.iter().map(|&c| c % next_mod).collect(),
            };

            // Lift self and current_inv to the larger modulus
            let a_lifted = self.reduce_mod(&lift_params);
            let x_lifted = current_inv.reduce_mod(&lift_params);

            // x' = x * (2 - a*x) mod next_mod
            let ax = a_lifted.mul(&x_lifted, &lift_params);
            let two = GRElement::from_int(2, &lift_params);
            let two_minus_ax = two.sub(&ax, &lift_params);
            current_inv = x_lifted.mul(&two_minus_ax, &lift_params);

            current_mod = next_mod;
        }

        // Final reduction mod p^s
        Some(current_inv.reduce_mod(params))
    }

    /// Reduce coefficients modulo a (possibly smaller) modulus.
    fn reduce_mod(&self, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self {
        let coeffs = self
            .coeffs
            .iter()
            .map(|&c| c % params.modulus)
            .collect();
        GRElement { coeffs }
    }

    /// Compute a^{p^r - 2} in GF(p^r) (used when s=1).
    /// This gives the inverse by Fermat's little theorem in the finite field.
    fn pow_in_field(&self, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self {
        debug_assert_eq!(params.s, 1);
        // Exponent: p^r - 2
        let order = pow_u128(params.p as u128, params.r) - 2;
        self.pow_u128(order, params)
    }

    /// Exponentiation by a u128 exponent (square-and-multiply).
    fn pow_u128(&self, mut exp: u128, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self {
        let mut result = GRElement::one(params);
        let mut base = self.clone();

        while exp > 0 {
            if exp & 1 == 1 {
                result = result.mul(&base, params);
            }
            exp >>= 1;
            if exp > 0 {
                base = base.mul(&base, params);
            }
        }
        result
    }

    /// Exponentiation by a u64 exponent.
    pub fn pow(&self, mut exp: u64, params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self {
        let mut result = GRElement::one(params);
        let mut base = self.clone();

        while exp > 0 {
            if exp & 1 == 1 {
                result = result.mul(&base, params);
            }
            exp >>= 1;
            if exp > 0 {
                base = base.mul(&base, params);
            }
        }
        result
    }

    // ------------------------------------------------------------------
    //  Serialization helpers
    // ------------------------------------------------------------------

    /// Serialize to bytes (for hashing / Merkle tree).
    pub fn to_bytes(&self) -> Vec<u8> {
        let mut bytes = Vec::with_capacity(self.coeffs.len() * 8);
        for &c in &self.coeffs {
            bytes.extend_from_slice(&c.to_le_bytes());
        }
        bytes
    }

    /// Deserialize from bytes.
    pub fn from_bytes(bytes: &[u8], params: &GaloisRingParams) -> Self {
        let r = params.r as usize;
        assert_eq!(bytes.len(), r * 8);
        let coeffs = (0..r)
            .map(|i| {
                let start = i * 8;
                u64::from_le_bytes(bytes[start..start + 8].try_into().unwrap()) % params.modulus
            })
            .collect();
        GRElement { coeffs }
    }
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
//  Display and Debug
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

impl fmt::Debug for GRElement {
    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {
        write!(f, "GRElement({:?})", self.coeffs)
    }
}

impl fmt::Display for GRElement {
    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {
        let mut first = true;
        for (i, &c) in self.coeffs.iter().enumerate() {
            if c == 0 {
                continue;
            }
            if !first {
                write!(f, " + ")?;
            }
            if i == 0 {
                write!(f, "{}", c)?;
            } else if c == 1 {
                write!(f, "x^{}", i)?;
            } else {
                write!(f, "{}*x^{}", c, i)?;
            }
            first = false;
        }
        if first {
            write!(f, "0")?;
        }
        Ok(())
    }
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
//  Utility
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

fn gcd_u64(a: u64, b: u64) -> u64 {
    let mut a = a;
    let mut b = b;
    while b != 0 {
        let t = b;
        b = a % b;
        a = t;
    }
    a
}

fn pow_u128(base: u128, exp: u32) -> u128 {
    let mut result = 1u128;
    for _ in 0..exp {
        result = result.checked_mul(base).expect("overflow in pow_u128");
    }
    result
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
//  Tests
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;
    use rand::rngs::StdRng;
    use rand::SeedableRng;

    fn z4_params() -> GaloisRingParams {
        // GR(2^2, 1) = Z_4
        GaloisRingParams::new(2, 2, 1, vec![0])
    }

    fn gf4_params() -> GaloisRingParams {
        // GR(2^1, 2) = GF(4) = GF(2)[x]/(x^2 + x + 1)
        GaloisRingParams::new(2, 1, 2, vec![1, 1])
    }

    fn gr4_2_params() -> GaloisRingParams {
        // GR(2^2, 2) = Z_4[x]/(x^2 + x + 1), 16 elements
        GaloisRingParams::new(2, 2, 2, vec![1, 1])
    }

    fn gf9_params() -> GaloisRingParams {
        // GR(3^1, 2) = GF(9) = GF(3)[x]/(x^2 + 1)
        GaloisRingParams::new(3, 1, 2, vec![1, 0])
    }

    // ---- Z_4 tests ----

    #[test]
    fn test_z4_add() {
        let p = z4_params();
        let a = GRElement::from_int(3, &p);
        let b = GRElement::from_int(2, &p);
        let c = a.add(&b, &p);
        assert_eq!(c.coeffs[0], 1); // 3 + 2 = 5 mod 4 = 1
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_z4_mul() {
        let p = z4_params();
        let a = GRElement::from_int(3, &p);
        let b = GRElement::from_int(3, &p);
        let c = a.mul(&b, &p);
        assert_eq!(c.coeffs[0], 1); // 3 * 3 = 9 mod 4 = 1
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_z4_units() {
        let p = z4_params();
        assert!(GRElement::from_int(1, &p).is_unit(&p));
        assert!(GRElement::from_int(3, &p).is_unit(&p));
        assert!(!GRElement::from_int(0, &p).is_unit(&p));
        assert!(!GRElement::from_int(2, &p).is_unit(&p));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_z4_zero_divisor() {
        let p = z4_params();
        // 2 is a zero divisor in Z_4: 2 * 2 = 0
        let two = GRElement::from_int(2, &p);
        assert!(two.is_zero_divisor(&p));
        let prod = two.mul(&two, &p);
        assert!(prod.is_zero());
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_z4_inv() {
        let p = z4_params();
        let a = GRElement::from_int(3, &p);
        let inv = a.inv(&p).unwrap();
        let prod = a.mul(&inv, &p);
        assert_eq!(prod, GRElement::one(&p)); // 3 * 3 = 1 mod 4
    }

    // ---- GF(4) tests ----

    #[test]
    fn test_gf4_all_nonzero_are_units() {
        let p = gf4_params();
        // GF(4) is a field: every nonzero element is a unit.
        // Elements: 0, 1, x, x+1 (where x^2 = x + 1)
        for a0 in 0..2u64 {
            for a1 in 0..2u64 {
                let e = GRElement::new(vec![a0, a1], &p);
                if !e.is_zero() {
                    assert!(e.is_unit(&p), "nonzero {:?} should be a unit in GF(4)", e);
                }
            }
        }
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_gf4_mul() {
        let p = gf4_params();
        // x * x = x^2 = x + 1 (since x^2 + x + 1 = 0 → x^2 = -x - 1 = x + 1 in GF(2))
        let x = GRElement::new(vec![0, 1], &p);
        let x2 = x.mul(&x, &p);
        assert_eq!(x2, GRElement::new(vec![1, 1], &p));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_gf4_inv() {
        let p = gf4_params();
        // Verify that a * a^{-1} = 1 for all nonzero elements.
        for a0 in 0..2u64 {
            for a1 in 0..2u64 {
                let e = GRElement::new(vec![a0, a1], &p);
                if !e.is_zero() {
                    let inv = e.inv(&p).unwrap();
                    let prod = e.mul(&inv, &p);
                    assert_eq!(prod, GRElement::one(&p), "inv failed for {:?}", e);
                }
            }
        }
    }

    // ---- GR(4, 2) tests ----

    #[test]
    fn test_gr4_2_unit_inv() {
        let p = gr4_2_params();
        let a = GRElement::new(vec![1, 1], &p); // 1 + x
        // gcd(1, 1, 4) = 1, so it's a unit.
        assert!(a.is_unit(&p));
        let inv = a.inv(&p).unwrap();
        let prod = a.mul(&inv, &p);
        assert_eq!(prod, GRElement::one(&p));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_gr4_2_zero_divisor() {
        let p = gr4_2_params();
        // 2 * (1 + x) = 2 + 2x. This is in the ideal (2), so it's a zero divisor.
        let two_plus_2x = GRElement::new(vec![2, 2], &p);
        assert!(!two_plus_2x.is_unit(&p));
        assert!(two_plus_2x.is_zero_divisor(&p));
        assert_eq!(two_plus_2x.gcd_with_modulus(&p), 2);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_gr4_2_ideal_class() {
        let p = gr4_2_params();
        assert_eq!(GRElement::zero(&p).ideal_class(&p), 2); // s = 2
        assert_eq!(GRElement::one(&p).ideal_class(&p), 0); // unit
        assert_eq!(GRElement::new(vec![2, 0], &p).ideal_class(&p), 1); // in (2) but not zero
    }

    // ---- GF(9) tests ----

    #[test]
    fn test_gf9_inv() {
        let p = gf9_params();
        // Test all nonzero elements are invertible (it's a field).
        let mut count = 0;
        for a0 in 0..3u64 {
            for a1 in 0..3u64 {
                let e = GRElement::new(vec![a0, a1], &p);
                if !e.is_zero() {
                    count += 1;
                    let inv = e.inv(&p).unwrap();
                    let prod = e.mul(&inv, &p);
                    assert_eq!(
                        prod,
                        GRElement::one(&p),
                        "inv failed for {:?} in GF(9)",
                        e
                    );
                }
            }
        }
        assert_eq!(count, 8); // GF(9) has 8 nonzero elements
    }

    // ---- Property tests ----

    #[test]
    fn test_ring_axioms_gr4_2() {
        let p = gr4_2_params();
        let mut rng = StdRng::seed_from_u64(42);

        for _ in 0..100 {
            let a = GRElement::random(&mut rng, &p);
            let b = GRElement::random(&mut rng, &p);
            let c = GRElement::random(&mut rng, &p);

            // Commutativity of addition
            assert_eq!(a.add(&b, &p), b.add(&a, &p));

            // Commutativity of multiplication
            assert_eq!(a.mul(&b, &p), b.mul(&a, &p));

            // Associativity of multiplication
            let ab_c = a.mul(&b, &p).mul(&c, &p);
            let a_bc = a.mul(&b.mul(&c, &p), &p);
            assert_eq!(ab_c, a_bc);

            // Distributivity: a*(b+c) = a*b + a*c
            let lhs = a.mul(&b.add(&c, &p), &p);
            let rhs = a.mul(&b, &p).add(&a.mul(&c, &p), &p);
            assert_eq!(lhs, rhs);

            // Additive identity
            let zero = GRElement::zero(&p);
            assert_eq!(a.add(&zero, &p), a);

            // Multiplicative identity
            let one = GRElement::one(&p);
            assert_eq!(a.mul(&one, &p), a);

            // Additive inverse
            let neg_a = a.neg(&p);
            assert!(a.add(&neg_a, &p).is_zero());
        }
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_all_units_invertible_gr4_2() {
        let p = gr4_2_params();
        // Exhaustively check all 16 elements
        let mut unit_count = 0;
        for a0 in 0..4u64 {
            for a1 in 0..4u64 {
                let e = GRElement::new(vec![a0, a1], &p);
                if e.is_unit(&p) {
                    unit_count += 1;
                    let inv = e.inv(&p).expect("unit should be invertible");
                    let prod = e.mul(&inv, &p);
                    assert_eq!(prod, GRElement::one(&p), "inv failed for {:?}", e);
                }
            }
        }
        // |units| = p^{sr} - p^{(s-1)r} = 4^2 - 2^2 = 16 - 4 = 12
        assert_eq!(unit_count, 12);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_random_unit() {
        let p = gr4_2_params();
        let mut rng = StdRng::seed_from_u64(123);
        for _ in 0..50 {
            let u = GRElement::random_unit(&mut rng, &p);
            assert!(u.is_unit(&p));
        }
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_serialization_roundtrip() {
        let p = gr4_2_params();
        let mut rng = StdRng::seed_from_u64(99);
        for _ in 0..20 {
            let e = GRElement::random(&mut rng, &p);
            let bytes = e.to_bytes();
            let e2 = GRElement::from_bytes(&bytes, &p);
            assert_eq!(e, e2);
        }
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_display() {
        let p = gr4_2_params();
        let e = GRElement::new(vec![3, 2], &p);
        let s = format!("{}", e);
        assert!(s.contains("3"));
        assert!(s.contains("x^1"));
    }
}
```

最后是模块入口文件：

```rust name=src/galois_ring/mod.rs
//! Galois ring GR(p^s, r) arithmetic.
//!
//! This module implements the algebraic structure described in §2.1 of
//! "Transparent SNARKs over Galois Rings" (Wei, Zhang, Deng).

pub mod ring;
pub mod element;

pub use ring::GaloisRingParams;
pub use element::GRElement;
```

---

### 设计要点说明

**`ring.rs` 核心逻辑**

| 功能 | 对应论文内容 |
|------|-------------|
| `new_auto()` | 自动查找 GF(p) 上 r 次不可约多项式（Fact 4：GF(p,r) 上不可约 → GR(p^s,r) 上不可约） |
| `is_irreducible_mod_p()` | 标准算法：检查 $x^{p^r} \equiv x \pmod{f}$ 且对所有 $i < r$ 有 $\gcd(x^{p^i} - x, f) = 1$ |
| `is_large_ring()` | 判断 $p^r \geq 2^{127}$，决定走 Algorithm 1 还是 Algorithm 2 |
| `extension_degree()` | 计算小环扩展倍数 $k$，使得 $p^{kr} \geq 2^{127}$ |

**`element.rs` 核心逻辑**

| 功能 | 对应论文内容 |
|------|-------------|
| `mul()` | 多项式乘法 + 对 $f(x)$ 取模，系数运算 mod $p^s$ |
| `gcd_with_modulus()` | **Definition 2**: $\gcd(a, p^s) = \gcd(a_0, \ldots, a_{r-1}, p^s)$ |
| `is_unit()` | **Fact 1**: 不在 $(p)$ 中 ⟺ gcd = 1 ⟺ 可逆 |
| `ideal_class()` | §3.1 码距分析中对零因子按 $(p^{s-1}), \ldots, (p)$ 分类 |
| `inv()` | **Fact 2 推论**: gcd = 1 时可逆。用 Hensel lifting: 先在 GF(p^r) 中求逆，再逐步提升到 $\mathbb{Z}_{p^s}$ |

**Hensel Lifting 求逆的原理**：
1. 先在 $\text{GF}(p^r)$ 中用 Fermat 小定理求 $a^{-1} \equiv a^{p^r - 2}$
2. 利用 Newton 迭代 $x' = x(2 - ax)$，每次将精度从 mod $p^k$ 提升到 mod $p^{2k}$
3. 经过 $O(\log s)$ 轮迭代得到 mod $p^s$ 下的逆

## @Entropy-pp

我觉得可以不用 rust ，参考 https://github.com/aucrypto/rinocchio/tree/master ，这也是一个类似方案的实现，它是用 C++实现的，请你仔细阅读这个代码库，给我一个新的实现我的论文的思路

## Copilot

我已经完整读完了 Rinocchio 代码库。下面给你一个完整的对比分析和新的实现方案。

---

## Rinocchio 代码库架构解剖

先看清楚 Rinocchio 的**技术栈选型与模块设计**：

| 文件 | 职责 | 核心依赖 |
|------|------|----------|
| `gr.h/cpp` | Galois Ring 算术：随机可逆元、例外集、求逆、不可约多项式 | **NTL 库** (`ZZ_pE`) |
| `circuit.h/cpp` | 算术电路定义与求值 | STL |
| `qrp.h/cpp` | QRP (Quadratic Ring Program)：Circuit → 多项式 V,W,Y,t | NTL (`ZZ_pEX`) |
| `joye_libert.h/cpp` | Joye-Libert 同态加密方案 (充当"编码"角色) | NTL (`ZZ`) |
| `setup.h/cpp` | 可信设置：生成 SecretState + CRS | 所有上层模块 |
| `rinocchio.h/cpp` | Prove / Verify 核心流程 | 所有模块 |

**Rinocchio 的关键设计决策：**

1. **用 NTL 库做一切 Galois Ring 算术** —— `ZZ_p` 是 $\mathbb{Z}_{p^s}$，`ZZ_pE` 是 $\mathbb{Z}_{p^s}[x]/(f(x))$ 即 $\text{GR}(p^s, r)$，`ZZ_pEX` 是 Galois Ring 上的单变量多项式。NTL 直接提供了加/减/乘/除/求值/插值/GCD，不需要自己写。
2. **求逆用 XGCD** —— 把元素提升到 $\mathbb{Z}[x]$ 做扩展欧几里得，而非 Hensel lifting。
3. **不可约多项式用查表** —— 硬编码了 degree 2~32 以及 40/60/80 的本原不可约多项式。
4. **代码量极小** —— 总共 ~40KB，C++11，结构清晰。

---

## 你的论文 vs Rinocchio：根本差异

| 维度 | Rinocchio | 你的论文 (Brakedown over GR) |
|------|-----------|------------------------------|
| **框架** | Linear PCP (Pinocchio/Groth16 路线) | PIOP + Polynomial Commitment |
| **SRS** | ❌ 需要可信设置 (Trusted Setup) | ✅ 透明 (Transparent)，无 SRS |
| **密码学原语** | Joye-Libert 同态加密 | 仅抗碰撞哈希函数 |
| **多项式处理** | 单变量多项式 QRP：V(x)·W(x)-Y(x)=H(x)·t(x) | 多线性多项式 + 矩阵布局 |
| **核心机制** | 加密求值：$E(f(s))$ | 线性码编码 + Merkle 承诺 + Testing |
| **电路模型** | 算术电路 → QRP | 多线性多项式的 commitment + evaluation |

**关键结论**：你**不能**直接照搬 Rinocchio 的 `setup/prove/verify` 框架，但**应该**照搬它对 NTL 的使用方式——NTL 直接提供了 Galois Ring 算术，省掉你自己写环算术的工作。

---

## 新的实现方案：C++ / NTL

### 技术选型

```
语言:        C++17
代数库:      NTL (与 Rinocchio 相同)
             ZZ_p  → Z_{p^s} 的系数
             ZZ_pE → GR(p^s, r) 的元素
             ZZ_pEX → GR 上的多项式 (sumcheck 用)
哈希:        OpenSSL SHA-256 或自带简单实现
构建:        CMake (比 Rinocchio 的裸 Makefile 更好管理)
```

### 项目结构

```
brakedown-gr/
├── CMakeLists.txt
├── README.md
│
├── include/
│   ├── gr.h                 # [照搬+扩展] Galois Ring 工具函数
│   ├── params.h             # Galois Ring 参数 + 编码参数
│   ├── linear_code.h        # 线性码: Expander Code over GR
│   ├── multilinear.h        # 多线性多项式
│   ├── merkle.h             # Merkle 树
│   ├── transcript.h         # Fiat-Shamir transcript
│   ├── poly_commit.h        # Brakedown 多项式承诺 (核心)
│   └── hash.h               # 哈希函数封装
│
├── src/
│   ├── gr.cpp               # [照搬+扩展] 环算术 
│   ├── params.cpp           # 参数初始化
│   ├── linear_code.cpp      # Expander Code 编码
│   ├── multilinear.cpp      # 多线性多项式操作
│   ├── merkle.cpp           # Merkle 树构建/验证
│   ├── transcript.cpp       # Fiat-Shamir
│   ├── poly_commit.cpp      # Commit / Eval / Verify 完整协议
│   └── hash.cpp             # SHA-256 封装
│
├── test/
│   ├── test_gr.cpp          # 环算术测试
│   ├── test_code.cpp        # 编码测试
│   ├── test_merkle.cpp      # Merkle 树测试
│   └── test_commit.cpp      # 端到端承诺测试 (main)
│
└── bench/
    └── bench_commit.cpp     # 性能测试
```

### 各模块详细设计

#### 1. `gr.h / gr.cpp` — 从 Rinocchio 照搬并扩展

直接复用 Rinocchio 的模式，保持 NTL 的 `ZZ_pE` 作为核心类型：

```cpp name=include/gr.h
#ifndef GR_H
#define GR_H

#include <NTL/ZZ_pE.h>
#include <NTL/ZZ_pEX.h>

using namespace NTL;

// ============================================================
//  以下直接借鉴 Rinocchio gr.h，GR(p^s, r) 基础操作
// ============================================================

// 初始化 GR(p^s, r): 设置 ZZ_p 的模数为 p^s, ZZ_pE 的模多项式
void initGaloisRing(long p, long s, long r);

// 从 Rinocchio 照搬：随机可逆元 (不在 ideal (p) 中)
ZZ_pE randomInvertible();

// 从 Rinocchio 照搬：例外集 (元素间差可逆)
ZZ_pE indexedElementInExceptionalSet(long index);
Vec<ZZ_pE> getExceptionalSubset(long size);
ZZ_pE randomInExceptionalSet();
ZZ_pE randomNonZeroInExceptionalSet();

// 从 Rinocchio 照搬：用 XGCD 求逆
ZZ_pE getInverse(ZZ_pE element);

// 从 Rinocchio 照搬：不可约多项式查表
ZZ_pX primitiveIrredPoly(long degree);

// ============================================================
//  以下是你的论文额外需要的，Rinocchio 没有的
// ============================================================

// Definition 2: gcd(a, p^s) = gcd(a_0, ..., a_{r-1}, p^s)
long gcdWithModulus(const ZZ_pE& a, long p, long s);

// Fact 1: 判断是否为零因子 (在 ideal (p) 中)
bool isZeroDivisor(const ZZ_pE& a, long p);

// 零因子的理想类别: 最大的 i 使得 a ∈ (p^i)
int idealClass(const ZZ_pE& a, long p, long s);

// 判断环是否为 "大环": p^r >= 2^securityBits
bool isLargeRing(long p, long r, long securityBits = 127);

// 计算扩展倍数 k
long extensionDegree(long p, long r, long securityBits = 127);

// 小环扩展: 初始化 GR(p^s, kr) 作为 GR(p^s, r) 的扩展
// 返回 k 次不可约多项式
void initExtendedRing(long p, long s, long r, long k);

#endif
```

#### 2. `params.h` — 统一参数管理

```cpp name=include/params.h
#ifndef PARAMS_H
#define PARAMS_H

#include <NTL/ZZ_pE.h>
using namespace NTL;

// Galois Ring 全局参数
struct GRParams {
    long p;          // 素数
    long s;          // 特征指数
    long r;          // 不可约多项式次数
    long k;          // 扩展倍数 (大环时 k=1)
    long modulus;    // p^s
    long securityParam; // λ
};

// Expander Code 参数 (对应论文 Table 1)
struct CodeParams {
    double alpha;
    double beta;
    double t;        // 编码扩展比
    long c_n;        // A 矩阵每行非零个数
    long d_n;        // B 矩阵每行非零个数
    long n0;         // 递归终止阈值
    double rate;     // 码率 = 1/t
    double distance; // 相对码距
};

// 根据 n 和 GR 参数选择 Code 参数
CodeParams selectCodeParams(long n, const GRParams& gr);

// Brakedown 多项式承诺的公共参数
struct PublicParams {
    GRParams gr;
    CodeParams code;
    long numVars;    // μ, 多线性多项式变元数
    long m;          // 系数矩阵行数 = 2^{μ/2}
    long n;          // 系数矩阵列数 = 2^{ceil(μ/2)}
    long lQ;         // Testing phase 查询次数 = Θ(λ)
};

PublicParams setupParams(long securityParam, long numVars, 
                          long p, long s, long r);

#endif
```

#### 3. `linear_code.h` — Expander Code (论文 §3)

```cpp name=include/linear_code.h
#ifndef LINEAR_CODE_H
#define LINEAR_CODE_H

#include <NTL/ZZ_pE.h>
#include <NTL/matrix.h>
#include <vector>
#include "params.h"

using namespace NTL;

// 稀疏矩阵: 每行 d 个非零项
struct SparseRow {
    std::vector<long> colIndices;  // 非零列下标
    std::vector<ZZ_pE> values;    // 对应的非零值
};

struct SparseMatrix {
    long rows, cols;
    std::vector<SparseRow> data;
};

// 采样 M_{n,m,d}: 每行 d 个随机非零项
SparseMatrix sampleSparseMatrix(long rows, long cols, long d);

// 稀疏矩阵-向量乘
Vec<ZZ_pE> sparseMul(const SparseMatrix& M, const Vec<ZZ_pE>& x);

// ============================================================
//  Algorithm 1: Enc (大环 / 扩展后的环)
//  GR(p^s, r)^n  →  GR(p^s, r)^{tn}
// ============================================================
struct ExpanderCode {
    CodeParams params;
    long n;                         // 输入长度
    std::vector<SparseMatrix> As;   // 各递归层的 A 矩阵
    std::vector<SparseMatrix> Bs;   // 各递归层的 B 矩阵
    Mat<ZZ_pE> baseMatrix;          // n < n0 时的生成矩阵
};

// 预处理: 生成编码所需的所有随机矩阵
ExpanderCode setupExpanderCode(long n, const CodeParams& params);

// 编码: x → w = (x, z, v)
Vec<ZZ_pE> encode(const ExpanderCode& code, const Vec<ZZ_pE>& x);

// ============================================================
//  Algorithm 2: Enc' (小环)
//  将 k 个 GR(p^s,r) 元素视为 1 个 GR(p^s,kr) 元素后编码
// ============================================================

// 打包: k 个小环元素 → 1 个大环元素
ZZ_pE packElements(const Vec<ZZ_pE>& elems, long k);

// 解包: 1 个大环元素 → k 个小环元素
Vec<ZZ_pE> unpackElement(const ZZ_pE& elem, long k);

// 小环编码
Vec<ZZ_pE> encodeExtended(const ExpanderCode& code, 
                           const Vec<ZZ_pE>& x, long k);

#endif
```

#### 4. `multilinear.h` — 多线性多项式 (论文 §1.2 的矩阵布局)

```cpp name=include/multilinear.h
#ifndef MULTILINEAR_H
#define MULTILINEAR_H

#include <NTL/ZZ_pE.h>
#include "params.h"

using namespace NTL;

// μ-变元多线性多项式, 存储 2^μ 个求值
struct MultilinearPoly {
    long numVars;           // μ
    Vec<ZZ_pE> evals;      // 长度 2^μ, 在 {0,1}^μ 上的值
};

// 在任意点 r ∈ GR^μ 处求值
ZZ_pE evaluate(const MultilinearPoly& poly, const Vec<ZZ_pE>& r);

// 将 2^μ 个系数排列成矩阵 U: m×n
// m = 2^{μ/2}, n = 2^{ceil(μ/2)}
struct CoefficientMatrix {
    long m, n;              // 行数, 列数
    Mat<ZZ_pE> data;        // m × n 矩阵
};

CoefficientMatrix toMatrix(const MultilinearPoly& poly);

// 计算 s1 和 s2 向量 (论文 §1.2):
//   s1 = (1-r1, r1) ⊗ ... ⊗ (1-r_{l/2}, r_{l/2})
//   s2 = (1-r_{l/2+1}, r_{l/2+1}) ⊗ ... ⊗ (1-r_l, r_l)
// 使得 f(r) = s1^T * U * s2
Vec<ZZ_pE> computeTensorLeft(const Vec<ZZ_pE>& r, long numVars);
Vec<ZZ_pE> computeTensorRight(const Vec<ZZ_pE>& r, long numVars);

#endif
```

#### 5. `poly_commit.h` — 核心：Brakedown 多项式承诺 (论文 §4)

```cpp name=include/poly_commit.h
#ifndef POLY_COMMIT_H
#define POLY_COMMIT_H

#include <NTL/ZZ_pE.h>
#include "params.h"
#include "linear_code.h"
#include "multilinear.h"
#include "merkle.h"
#include "transcript.h"

using namespace NTL;

// ============================================================
//  数据结构
// ============================================================

// 承诺 (公开)
struct Commitment {
    unsigned char merkleRoot[32];  // Û 各列的 Merkle 根
};

// 承诺时 Prover 保存的私有状态
struct CommitState {
    CoefficientMatrix U;           // 系数矩阵
    Mat<ZZ_pE> encodedU;           // 编码后矩阵 Û (m 行, 每行编码)
    MerkleTree tree;               // 对 Û 各列的 Merkle 树
    ExpanderCode code;             // 编码实例
};

// Testing Phase 的证据
struct TestingProof {
    Mat<ZZ_pE> V;                  // V = R·U, k×(m/k) 矩阵
    std::vector<long> querySet;    // Q ⊂ [tm/k], |Q| = l_Q
    // 对于每个 j ∈ Q:
    std::vector<Vec<ZZ_pE>> queriedColumns;  // Û 的第 j 列
    std::vector<MerkleProof> merkleProofs;   // 对应的 Merkle 路径
};

// Eval Phase 的证据
struct EvalProof {
    Vec<ZZ_pE> w;                  // q1^T · Û
    TestingProof testingProof;     // Testing Phase 证据
};

// ============================================================
//  API: Gen / Commit / Eval-Prove / Eval-Verify
// ============================================================

// Gen: 生成公共参数
PublicParams gen(long securityParam, long numVars, 
                 long p, long s, long r);

// Commit: 承诺多线性多项式
// 返回 (公开承诺, Prover 私有状态)
std::pair<Commitment, CommitState> commit(
    const PublicParams& pp,
    const MultilinearPoly& poly);

// Eval-Prove: Prover 证明 poly(z) = v
EvalProof evalProve(
    const PublicParams& pp,
    const Commitment& comm,
    const CommitState& state,
    const Vec<ZZ_pE>& z,          // 求值点
    const ZZ_pE& v,               // 声称的值
    Transcript& transcript);

// Eval-Verify: Verifier 验证
bool evalVerify(
    const PublicParams& pp,
    const Commitment& comm,
    const Vec<ZZ_pE>& z,
    const ZZ_pE& v,
    const EvalProof& proof,
    Transcript& transcript);

#endif
```

#### 6. `merkle.h` / `transcript.h` — 基础设施

```cpp name=include/merkle.h
#ifndef MERKLE_H
#define MERKLE_H

#include <NTL/ZZ_pE.h>
#include <vector>
#include "hash.h"

using namespace NTL;

struct MerkleProof {
    long leafIndex;
    std::vector<unsigned char[32]> path; // 兄弟节点哈希
};

struct MerkleTree {
    unsigned char root[32];
    std::vector<std::vector<unsigned char>> nodes;
    long numLeaves;
};

// 对一组列 (每列是一个 Vec<ZZ_pE>) 构建 Merkle 树
MerkleTree buildMerkleTree(const std::vector<Vec<ZZ_pE>>& columns);

// 生成第 index 列的 Merkle 路径
MerkleProof openMerkle(const MerkleTree& tree, long index);

// 验证 Merkle 路径
bool verifyMerkle(const unsigned char root[32],
                  const MerkleProof& proof,
                  const Vec<ZZ_pE>& leaf);

#endif
```

```cpp name=include/transcript.h
#ifndef TRANSCRIPT_H
#define TRANSCRIPT_H

#include <NTL/ZZ_pE.h>
#include <vector>
#include "hash.h"

using namespace NTL;

// Fiat-Shamir Transcript: 交互式 → 非交互式
class Transcript {
public:
    Transcript(const std::string& label);
    
    void appendMessage(const std::string& label, 
                       const unsigned char* data, long len);
    void appendElement(const std::string& label, const ZZ_pE& elem);
    
    // 从 GR(p^s, r) 中抽取随机挑战
    ZZ_pE challengeElement(const std::string& label);
    
    // 抽取随机矩阵 R ∈ GR^{rows × cols} (Testing Phase 用)
    Mat<ZZ_pE> challengeMatrix(const std::string& label, 
                                long rows, long cols);
    
    // 抽取随机子集 Q ⊂ [n], |Q| = size
    std::vector<long> challengeIndexSet(const std::string& label,
                                         long size, long n);

private:
    std::vector<unsigned char> state;
    void squeeze(unsigned char* out, long len);
};

#endif
```

### CMakeLists.txt

```cmake name=CMakeLists.txt
cmake_minimum_required(VERSION 3.16)
project(brakedown-gr LANGUAGES CXX)

set(CMAKE_CXX_STANDARD 17)
set(CMAKE_CXX_STANDARD_REQUIRED ON)

# NTL + GMP (与 Rinocchio 相同的依赖)
find_library(NTL_LIB ntl REQUIRED)
find_library(GMP_LIB gmp REQUIRED)
find_package(OpenSSL REQUIRED) # for SHA-256

include_directories(include)

# 核心库
add_library(brakedown_gr
    src/gr.cpp
    src/params.cpp
    src/linear_code.cpp
    src/multilinear.cpp
    src/merkle.cpp
    src/transcript.cpp
    src/poly_commit.cpp
    src/hash.cpp
)
target_link_libraries(brakedown_gr ${NTL_LIB} ${GMP_LIB} OpenSSL::Crypto)

# 测试
add_executable(test_commit test/test_commit.cpp)
target_link_libraries(test_commit brakedown_gr)

add_executable(test_gr test/test_gr.cpp)
target_link_libraries(test_gr brakedown_gr)

add_executable(test_code test/test_code.cpp)
target_link_libraries(test_code brakedown_gr)

# 性能测试
add_executable(bench_commit bench/bench_commit.cpp)
target_link_libraries(bench_commit brakedown_gr)
```

---

### 关键实现思路对比

下面对比 Rinocchio 的做法和你应该怎么做：

#### Galois Ring 算术

| Rinocchio 做法 | 你的做法 |
|----------------|----------|
| `ZZ_p::init(power(p, s))` 设置模数 | **一样** |
| `ZZ_pE::init(primitiveIrredPoly(r))` 设置商环 | **一样** |
| `randomInvertible()`: 检查至少一个系数是奇数 | **一样照搬** |
| `getInverse()`: XGCD | **一样照搬** |
| `primitiveIrredPoly()`: 查表 | **一样照搬** |
| 无 `gcdWithModulus` | **你需要新增**：遍历系数求 gcd，用于码距分析和 ideal class |

#### 编码层（Rinocchio 没有 ↔ 你的核心）

Rinocchio 用 Joye-Libert 加密取代了"承诺"，你完全不需要 `joye_libert.h/cpp`。取而代之的是：

```
Rinocchio: E(x) = JL-Encrypt(x)     → 同态加密, 需要密钥
你的论文:  C(x) = MerkleRoot(Enc(x)) → 哈希承诺, 无密钥 (透明)
```

所以你用 `linear_code + merkle` 取代 `joye_libert`。

#### Prove/Verify 对比

```
Rinocchio Prove:
  1. 计算 H(x) = (V·W - Y) / t
  2. 对 CRS 中的加密值做标量乘和同态加
  3. 输出 9 个 JLEncoding

你的 Prove (Eval Phase):
  1. 收到求值点 z, 计算 q1, q2 向量
  2. 计算 w = q1^T · Û (编码行的线性组合)
  3. 执行 Testing Phase:
     - Verifier 发 R, Prover 回 V = R·U
     - Verifier 抽查 Q 列, 验 Merkle + 线性组合一致性
  4. Verifier 解码 w 得到 q1^T·U, 与 q2 内积验证 f(z) = v
```

---

### 实现优先级路线图

```
Phase 1 (Week 1): 基础层
  ├── gr.cpp:  从 Rinocchio 移植 + 新增 gcdWithModulus / idealClass
  ├── params.cpp: 初始化函数
  ├── hash.cpp: SHA-256 封装
  └── test_gr.cpp: 验证 Z_4, GF(4), GR(4,2) 正确性

Phase 2 (Week 2): 编码层
  ├── linear_code.cpp: SparseMatrix + encode (Algorithm 1)
  ├── 小环扩展版 encodeExtended (Algorithm 2)
  └── test_code.cpp: 编码线性性测试

Phase 3 (Week 3): 承诺层
  ├── multilinear.cpp: 多线性多项式 + 矩阵布局
  ├── merkle.cpp: Merkle 树
  ├── transcript.cpp: Fiat-Shamir
  └── poly_commit.cpp: commit + evalProve + evalVerify 完整流程

Phase 4 (Week 4): 联调 + 性能
  ├── test_commit.cpp: 端到端测试
  ├── bench_commit.cpp: 性能测试
  └── 文档
```

---

### 一句话总结

> **环算术照搬 Rinocchio 的 NTL 用法 (`ZZ_pE`)，砍掉它的 `joye_libert` 和 `qrp`，换成你论文的 Expander Code + Merkle + Testing Phase。**

NTL 帮你把最难的 Galois Ring 算术全部搞定了（乘法、求逆、多项式运算），你专注在论文的真正新贡献上——编码和承诺协议。

要不要我先帮你把 `gr.cpp`（从 Rinocchio 移植+扩展）和 `params.cpp` 写出来？

## @Entropy-pp

我需要配置怎样的环境

## Copilot

好的，现在我根据 Rinocchio 的真实做法，结合你的项目需求，给你一份**完整详细的环境配置指南**。
